\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
M\+TC Call Interface Functions. 

This file includes call interface function. Those function is used to manage calls.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessATrsf()}{Mtc\_SessATrsf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+A\+Trsf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Trsf\+Sess }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC session attended transfer. 

If attended transfer successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a49e6136bd7de50a1a8451f0b4aea020e}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Trsf\+Acpt}}

If attended transfer failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a5cdef3f924f34531defcfab8cdf07db8}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Trsf\+Failed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a8745820d02835897c1120b8d9e7c8bae}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Trsf\+Term}}

while receiving attended transfer, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a28920432c7627f4e7f202035a047a785}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Refered}}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to make attended transfer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Trsf\+Sess} & The destination session to which you want to transfer this session.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
If you have a session with user A(indicated by i\+Sess\+Id) and a session with user B(indicated by i\+Trsf\+Sess\+Id), the result of attended transfer is A will have a session with B and all sessions you had with A and B will be terminated.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{mtc__call_8h_a51501510092e050a9252d1b872e84a3e}\label{mtc__call_8h_a51501510092e050a9252d1b872e84a3e}} 
\index{mtc\_call.h@{mtc\_call.h}!Mtc\_SessCall@{Mtc\_SessCall}}
\index{Mtc\_SessCall@{Mtc\_SessCall}!mtc\_call.h@{mtc\_call.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessCall()}{Mtc\_SessCall()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+U\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+C\+O\+N\+ST Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Z\+C\+O\+O\+K\+IE}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Video,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Add\+Ext }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC Call, establishing session call with video or audio. 

If send a new call and the callee answered, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}

If send a new call and the callee redirected, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7ed0936c87752443d17b079e4a913edb}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Outgoing}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}

If send a new call and the callee do not answered(timeout, busy now, etc.), G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa0ce0761081a423a5650337435381fb9}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Termed}}

While receiving call invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a84ef4abd17f6905ff80581ff472ccbdf}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Incoming}}.

While receiving call invitation and session is exist, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa5e2d289c20b03b34069e3ab15f08354}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Replaced}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to make a session call. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & Used to correspond session with UI resource. The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a54186075984a0bac8ac80fc3bf380cf7}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a9e93924137342028053729ad1afdf1b5}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Add\+Ext} & Indicate whether this call add extension header.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT, if return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT, should call Mtc\+\_\+\+Lcs\+Get\+Err\+Code 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a98cc54b4aab2670b1ad94d18348c03e4}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Answer}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a54186075984a0bac8ac80fc3bf380cf7}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a9e93924137342028053729ad1afdf1b5}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{mtc__call_8h_abd6e86e82be46c5d801c0feeb0a30f79}\label{mtc__call_8h_abd6e86e82be46c5d801c0feeb0a30f79}}

M\+TC Call, establishing session call with video or audio. 

If send a new call and the callee answered, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}

If send a new call and the callee redirected, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7ed0936c87752443d17b079e4a913edb}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Outgoing}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}

If send a new call and the callee do not answered(timeout, busy now, etc.), G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa0ce0761081a423a5650337435381fb9}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Termed}}

While receiving call invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a84ef4abd17f6905ff80581ff472ccbdf}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Incoming}}.

While receiving call invitation and session is exist, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa5e2d289c20b03b34069e3ab15f08354}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Replaced}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessEnableAdaptiveAspect()}{Mtc\_SessEnableAdaptiveAspect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Enable\+Adaptive\+Aspect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Enable,  }\item[{Z\+F\+L\+O\+AT}]{f\+Fixed\+Aspect }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC session enable/disable dynamic reset encoder to change video image aspect. The function should be called before \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a62330f465fc8ab1ed739c48a83c15d7e}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Camera\+Attach}}.

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em f\+Fixed\+Aspect,if} & $<$ 0 the outgoing video image will be adaptive the capture (camera, always 4\+:3) aspect, if =0 it will use codec settings(always 16\+:9, to be adaptive with the devices), if $>$0 will be with the setting fixed aspect(like 1.\+33, 1.\+77).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\em Z\+OK} & on successfully. \\
\hline

M\+TC session get called U\+RI and display name. Return P-\/\+Called-\/\+Party-\/\+ID header value in S\+IP invite message, other return TO header value. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ppc\+Uri} & The U\+RI of called party.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The caller must copy out parameter, then use.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
The called party information get by this function is actually from P-\/\+Called-\/\+Party-\/\+ID or TO header in S\+IP message. So the true identity of called user is not asserted by local U\+RI especially in the case of S\+IP gateway receiving an incoming call. \mbox{\Hypertarget{mtc__call_8h_a46b110af0fb8ec923084af52929d100d}\label{mtc__call_8h_a46b110af0fb8ec923084af52929d100d}}

M\+TC session get peer id, based on polices. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to get. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ppc\+Disp\+Name} & The display name of peer user which you have this session with. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ppc\+Uri} & The U\+RI of peer user which you have this session with.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The caller must copy out parameter, then use.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
Note the result of this function may be different with Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Peer\+Uri because the apply of polices. For example, O\+IP, O\+IR, T\+IP, T\+IR, and privacy.

The peer information get by this function is actually from F\+R\+O\+M/\+TO header in S\+IP message. So the true identity of peer user is not asserted by server.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessHold()}{Mtc\_SessHold()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Hold (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC session hold. 

If sending session hold successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a0f4d2896fa468956e546702db7809a4a}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Hold\+Ok}}

If sending session hold failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a0291c814dd0e96fc291aaa696ab98248}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Hold\+Failed}}

While receiving session held, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a1e2f744c1e0c4c2d67e7fdb31f61890c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Held}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to hold.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessPickUp()}{Mtc\_SessPickUp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+U\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Pick\+Up (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Replace\+Info,  }\item[{Z\+C\+O\+O\+K\+IE}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Video }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC Pick\+Up, establishing session call with video or audio by replacing specific call. 

If the new session call was accept by callee, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}.

If the new session call was reject by callee or no answer, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa0ce0761081a423a5650337435381fb9}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Termed}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to make a session call. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Replace\+Info} & The replace information used to locate replaced call. The format must comply with R\+F\+C3891, like \textquotesingle{}\href{mailto:425928@phone.example.org}{\texttt{ 425928@phone.\+example.\+org}};to-\/tag=7743;from-\/tag=6472\textquotesingle{}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & Used to correspond session with UI resource. The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a54186075984a0bac8ac80fc3bf380cf7}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a9e93924137342028053729ad1afdf1b5}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{mtc\_call.h@{mtc\_call.h}!Mtc\_SessRadioCall@{Mtc\_SessRadioCall}}
\index{Mtc\_SessRadioCall@{Mtc\_SessRadioCall}!mtc\_call.h@{mtc\_call.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessRadioCall()}{Mtc\_SessRadioCall()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+U\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Radio\+Call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+C\+O\+N\+ST Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$}]{pc\+Uri,  }\item[{Z\+C\+O\+O\+K\+IE}]{z\+Cookie,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Video,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Serv\+Info\+Type,  }\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Term\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC Call, establishing session call with video or audio. 

If send a new call and the callee answered, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}

If send a new call and the callee redirected, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7ed0936c87752443d17b079e4a913edb}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Outgoing}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a7c24ecb4dd0f6ed06a932a42cd94406c}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Talking}}

If send a new call and the callee do not answered(timeout, busy now, etc.), G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ac297651a626b8dd68be2b3d1f59a82f1}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Alerted}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa0ce0761081a423a5650337435381fb9}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Termed}}

While receiving call invitation, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a84ef4abd17f6905ff80581ff472ccbdf}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Incoming}}.

While receiving call invitation and session is exist, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa5e2d289c20b03b34069e3ab15f08354}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Replaced}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Uri} & The destination U\+RI to which you want to make a session call. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & Used to correspond session with UI resource. The cookie value could be get by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a54186075984a0bac8ac80fc3bf380cf7}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Get\+Cookie}} or reset by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a9e93924137342028053729ad1afdf1b5}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Set\+Cookie}} at any time of session\textquotesingle{}s life. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether this call has a voice stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether this call has a video stream. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Serv\+Info\+Type} & Indicate type of server info, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_a1fbaabb4ef8b4ead2b2ac358e0671207}{E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Term\+Type} & Indicate type of the seat terminal, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call_8h_afa915c71c305e8963effbb2b23b11134}{E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+T\+C\+\_\+\+T\+E\+R\+M\+I\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of this new created session on succeed, otherwise return Z\+M\+A\+X\+U\+I\+NT.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Loop} & Z\+F\+A\+L\+SE if play once. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Mix} & If false, microphone sound is replaced by file sound; if true, microphone sound is mixed with file sound\\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessUnhold()}{Mtc\_SessUnhold()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Unhold (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC session unhold. 

If sending session unhold successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a4a43bd5076bb86d0c1eb76a252487aae}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Un\+Hold\+Ok}}

If sending session hold failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ad84ebc0606e89ef2512a238186c24ac7}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Un\+Hold\+Failed}}

While receiving session unheld, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_acc18d6769ecb915474aaa97e43510029}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Un\+Held}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\

\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_SessUpdate()}{Mtc\_SessUpdate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Sess\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Audio,  }\item[{Z\+B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Video }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+TC session send a media update request to peer. The update in this function means open a new media stream or close an already exist media stream. 

If sending update successfully, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a0902f3050c167c41988f33255a8c1087}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Add\+Audio\+Ok}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ad7ec5c5ebbab4ef69a9ebb3a3f816814}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Rmv\+Audio\+Ok}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a30882b46bf16676d8ff0ab7126e31e9b}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Add\+Video\+Ok}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aa9acf8c14544000ec7fec87c4ffd6a4e}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Rmv\+Video\+Ok}}

If sending update failed, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a37329c68a463535409e969d5cfa2fb70}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Add\+Audio\+Failed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a09a0a4ba62599fd02d7dd3342d94adb9}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Rmv\+Audio\+Failed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_ad8ca7e8aa5cf0fc6958ccec2dce9caed}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Add\+Video\+Failed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a3d8317853118671fd39a34f78848f5f6}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Rmv\+Video\+Failed}}

While receiving update, G\+UI will be notified by callback which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a2666cb46807fce1c6f392638a696ed22}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Add\+Audio\+Req}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_aae4565cdeb267d628032c7ad0f2636b5}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Add\+Video\+Req}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The ID of session which you want to update its media. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Audio} & Indicate whether you want to have a audio stream after update. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em b\+Video} & Indicate whether you want to have a video stream after update.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & on succeed. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & on failure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
If the update request is accepted by peer, an indication will arise through the callback function which was set by \mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__call__cb_8h_a169bec3ef3079b38a23b0285cdc767c2}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Call\+Cb\+Set\+Mdfy\+Acpt}}.

After this operation, the session will be terminated by server.
